<small>(1993-present)</small>\n|website = [http://www.marthawash.com/ Official website]\n}}\n\n'''Martha Elaine Wash''' (born December 28, 1953) is a two time Grammy nominated American [[Contemporary R&B|R&B]], [[pop music|pop]], [[soul music|soul]], and [[house music|house]] [[singer]] and [[songwriter]] with a career spanning over thirty years. Known for her distinctive and powerful dramatic [[soprano]] voice.,<ref>{{cite news|last=Black|first=Sean|title=Favorable Forecast|url=http://aumag.org/wordpress/?p=3044|newspaper=A&U Magazine|date=January 16, 2012}}</ref> Wash first achieved fame as one half of the successful act [[The Weather Girls|Two Tons O' Fun]] who sang backing for the often dubbed ''Queen of Disco''<ref>{{cite news|author=APPublished: December 18, 1988 |url=http://query.nytimes.com/gst/fullpage.html?res=940DE0D8173EF93BA25751C1A96E948260 |title='&#39;The New York Times Obituaries'&#39; &#124; \"Sylvester, Singer and Entertainer, Dies at 42\" &#124; December 18, 1988 |publisher=New York Times |date=1988-12-18 |accessdate=2013-12-05}}</ref> [[Sylvester James|Sylvester]]. After gaining their own record deal, they released three consecutive commercially successful songs which all peaked at number 2 in the dance charts. The duo was renamed [[The Weather Girls]] in 1982 when they released the multi platinum single \"[[It's Raining Men]]\" in 1982 which brought the band to mainstream pop attention. After the  disbanding in 1985, Wash subsequently made a successful transition into House music as a featured artist on several successful songs. This has led her being branded as ''The Queen of Clubland''<ref>https://www.eventbrite.com/event/3974983282</ref> with seven Dance songs peaking at number one on the American Billboard Charts and a further four Dance songs peaking at number two, her most recent #1 song being the 2015 Tony Moran radio edit of \"Free People\"\n\nWash is also noted for spurring legislation in the 1990s that made vocal credits mandatory on CDs and music videos after being denied  proper credit (and royalties) for the million selling #1 song \"[[Gonna Make You Sweat (Everybody Dance Now)]]\" after she had been labeled \"unmarketable\" due to her weight."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"40146267":{"pageid":40146267,"ns":0,"title":"Martin Some other hits were \"It takes me away\" (Ger #3, 1994), \"Raveland\" (Ger #29, 1994), \"Deep\" (Ger #11, 1995), \"Unique\" (Ger #35, 1995), \"Secret\" (Ger #92, 1996), \"UR life\" (Ger #34, 1997), \"My best friend\" (Ger #73, 1997), \"Free love\" (Ger #97, 1998) and \"Ultimate sound\" (Ger #70, 1998).\nMarusha's career began in 1991 in Berlin with her radio programme \"Dancehall\" which went out each Saturday on the young people's station DT 64. When DT 64 had to close, Marusha changed the frequency and the name of her show. The Berlin station \"Fritz\" carried Marusha's \"Rave satellite\" once a week until 2007. To top this, the media multi-talent Marusha surprised German-speaking television audiences with \"Feuerreiter\", her TV programme for young people. For 2\u00bd years it was transmitted by [[Ostdeutscher Rundfunk Brandenburg|ORB]] and later [[ARD (broadcaster)|ARD]], and it was considered very popular."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"25085959":{"pageid":25085959,"ns":0,"title":"Masters At Work","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"#REDIRECT [[Masters at He produced the 1991 singles \u201cBeginning of Life\u201d and \u201cKeep Moving\u201d on Bassic Records.<ref>IMO Records. [http://www.imorecords.co.uk/house-2/house-artists/mike-perras-biography/ \"Mike Perras Biography\"], ''[[IMO Records]]' Retrieved on 14 March 2011.</ref>"}]}}}}{"warnings":{"main":{"*":"Unrecognized parameter: 'Sugar'"}},"query":{"normalized":[{"from":"Milk ","to":"Milk"}],"pages":{"19714":{"pageid":19714,"ns":0,"title":"Milk","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{about|the fluid produced by the mammary glands of mammals|milk derived from plants|Plant milk|other uses of the word|Milk&nbsp;(disambiguation)}}\n{{Use mdy dates|date=July 2014}}\n{{pp-semi-protected|small=yes}}{{pp-move-indef}}\n[[File:Milk glass.jpg|thumb|A glass of [[Pasteurization|pasteurized]] [[cattle|cow's]] milk]]'''Milk''' is a white liquid produced by the [[mammary gland]]s of [[mammal]]s. It is the primary source of [[nutrition]] for young mammals before they are able to [[digestion|digest]] other types of food. Early-[[lactation]] milk contains [[colostrum]], which carries the mother's [[antibody|antibodies]] to its young and can reduce the risk of many diseases. Milk contains many other nutrients<ref>{{cite journal|title=USDA's National Food and Nutrient Analysis Program: Food Sampling|author= Pehrsson, P.R.; Haytowitz, D.B.; Holden, J.M.; Perry, C.R. and Beckler, D.G. |journal=Journal of Food Composition and Analysis|year=2000|volume=13|pages=379\u2013389|doi=10.1006/jfca.1999.0867|url=http://www.nal.usda.gov/fnic/foodcomp/Data/Other/jfca13_379-389.pdf|archiveurl=http://web.archive.org/web/20030407085442/http://www.nal.usda.gov/fnic/foodcomp/Data/Other/jfca13_379-389.pdf|archivedate=April 7, 2003|issue=4}}</ref> and the carbohydrate [[lactose]]. The majority of the world's population is [[Lactose intolerance|lactose intolerant]].<ref>\"Only a relatively small percentage (about 30 percent) of the people in the world retain enough lactase to digest and absorb lactose efficiently throughout adult life.\" in {{cite book|author=Whitney, Ellie and Rolfes, Sharon Rady|title=Understanding Nutrition|isbn=978-1-133-60678-9|location=Belmont, CA|publisher=Wadsworth, Cengage Learning|year=2013|page=103}}</ref>\n\nAs an [[Agriculture|agricultural]] product, milk is [[Milking|extracted from mammals]] during or soon after pregnancy and is used as food for humans. Worldwide, [[dairy]] farms produced about 730 million tonnes of milk in 2011,<ref>{{cite web|title=Food Outlook \u2013 Global Market Analysis|date=May 2012|publisher=Food and Agriculture Organization of the United Nations|pages=8, 51\u201354|url=http://www.fao.org/docrep/015/al989e/al989e00.pdf}}</ref> from 260 million dairy cows.<ref>{{cite news |title=World Dairy Cow Numbers\n |url=http://www.dairyco.org.uk/market-information/farming-data/cow-numbers/world-cow-numbers/#.Uy6ZFM7Xehq\n |newspaper=[FAO]\n |date=January 14, 2014\n |accessdate=March 23, 2014}}</ref>  India is the world's largest producer and consumer of milk, yet neither exports nor imports it. New Zealand, the [[European Union]]'s 28 member states, Australia, and the United States are the world's largest exporters of milk and milk products. China and Russia are the world's largest importers of milk and milk products.<ref name=Blasko>{{cite web|url=http://ageconsearch.umn.edu/bitstream/104683/2/20_Blasko_PHD_Apstract.pdf|title=WORLD IMPORTANCE AND PRESENT TENDENCIES OF DAIRY SECTOR|author=Blasko, B.|work=University of Debrecen|year=2011}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|title=Food Outlook \u2013 Milk and Milk Products|publisher=FAO, United Nations|year=2010|url=http://www.fao.org/docrep/012/ak341e/ak341e10.htm}}</ref>\n\nThroughout the world, there are more than six billion consumers of milk and milk products. Over 750 million people live within dairy farming households.<ref>{{cite book|title=Status and Prospects for Smallholder Milk Production: A Global Perspective|publisher=Food and Agriculture Organization of the United Nations|year=2010|editor=Hemme, T. and Otte, J.|url=http://www.fao.org/docrep/012/i1522e/i1522e00.pdf}}</ref>"}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"2677821":{"pageid":2677821,"ns":0,"title":"Milton Jackson","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"'''Milton Jackson''' (real name '''Barry Christie''') is a [[music producer]] and  [[disc jockey|DJ]], specializing in [[Deep house]]. [[Armada Music|Armada]], [[Strictly Rhythm]], [[Spinnin' Records|Spinnin']]\n| associated_acts     = [[iiO]], [[Armin van Buuren]], [[Morgan Page]], [[Sultan & Ned Shepard]], [[Starkillers]]\n| website             = {{URL|nadiaali.com}}\n| current_members     =\n| past_members        =\n| notable_instruments =\n}}\n\n'''Nadia Ali''' ({{lang-ur|{{Nastaliq| \u0646\u0627\u062f\u06cc\u06c1 \u0639\u0644\u06cc}}}}) (born 3 August 1980) is a [[Pakistani American]] [[singer-songwriter]]. Ali gained prominence in 2001 as the [[frontwoman]] and songwriter of the band [[iiO]] after their debut single \"[[Rapture (iiO song)|Rapture]]\" reached No. 2 on the [[UK Singles Chart]].<ref name=OCC/> The song also charted across several countries in Europe.<ref name=iiO/> Their 2006 single, \"[[Is It Love?]]\", reached the top of the  ''[[Billboard (magazine)|Billboard]]'' [[Hot Dance Club Songs|Hot Dance Club Play Chart]].<ref name=BB/>\n\nAfter embarking on a solo career in 2005, Ali became successful as an oft-requested vocalist in [[electronic dance music]]. She released her debut album ''[[Embers (album)|Embers]]'' in 2009. Critics praised her unique songwriting, which combined [[electronica]] with [[Ballad (music)|ballads]], [[Eastern music|Eastern]] and [[acoustic music|acoustic]] music. Three singles from the album reached the top-ten of the ''Billboard'' Hot Dance Club Play Chart, including the No. 1 hit, \"[[Love Story (Nadia Ali song)|Love Story]]\".<ref name=BB1/><ref name=BB2/><ref name=BB3/> The song was also nominated at the 25th International Dance Music Awards at the [[Winter Music Conference]], while \"[[Fantasy (Nadia Ali song)|Fantasy]]\" was nominated for a [[Grammy]] award.<ref name=IDMA/><ref name=grammy/>\n\nIn 2010, she released a remix compilation titled ''Queen of Clubs Trilogy'' to mark her decade-long career as a singer-songwriter. \"Rapture\" was re-released as the only single from the compilation and the song was once again a chart success in Europe.<ref name=Romania/> Ali released the single \"[[Pressure (Nadia Ali song)|Pressure]]\" with Starkillers and Alex Kenji in 2011, which became a club and festival anthem and received an International Dance Music Award.<ref name=IDMA2/> In 2012, she collaborated with [[BT (musician)|BT]] and [[Arty (musician)|Arty]] on the single \"Must Be The Love\", which was nominated for an International Dance Music Award.<ref name=IDMA3/> She has also collaborated with several notable producers and DJs, such as [[Armin van Buuren]], [[Schiller (band)|Schiller]], [[Avicii]] and [[John Creamer & Stephane K]]. Ali is currently working on her second studio album, titled ''Phoenix''."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"8032843":{"pageid":8032843,"ns":0,"title":"Nadirah Shakoor","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{BLP sources|date=July 2011}}\n[[Image:nadirah shakoor.jpg|250px|thumb|Nadirah Shakoor performs with Jimmy Buffett's Coral Reefer Band in June 2009.]]\n\n'''Nadirah Shakoor''' is an [[United States|American]] [[vocalist]],<ref>{{cite news|url=http://books.google.com/books?id=9AsEAAAAMBAJ&pg=RA1-PA72&dq=Nadirah+Shakoor&hl=en&ei=ZtAtTqusNqnKiALR-divAg&sa=X&oi=book_result&ct=result&resnum=7&ved=0CEYQ6AEwBg#v=onepage&q=Nadirah%20Shakoor&f=false|title=Chrysilis/EMI solo artist speaks out|last=Nelson|first=Havelock|date=May 11, 1996|work=[[Billboard (magazine)|Billboard]]|page=72|accessdate=25 July 2011}}</ref> best known for her work in [[Jimmy Buffett]]'s [[Coral Reefer Band]], which she joined in 1995, and is still touring with it as its featured female vocalist. \"Nod to the Storyteller\" is Nadirah's tribute to Jimmy Buffett, who for the last 13 years has featured her as part of his show. Prior to that, she was a female vocalist of the hip hop group [[Arrested Development (hip hop group)|Arrested Development]], of which she was a member from 1993 until 1995. She was nominated for a [[Grammy Award]] for its second album, ''[[Zingalamaduni]]''. Nadirah was also featured in Arrested Development's ''[[Unplugged (Arrested Development album)|Unplugged]]'' DVD and album. She also toured or recorded with [[Madonna (entertainer)|Madonna]], [[Al Jarreau]], [[Paula Abdul]], [[Quincy Jones]], [[Jasmine Guy]], Howard Hewit, and others.\n\nHer debut album, \"Soul Power\" (EMI Music Japan), was produced by [[Speech (rapper)|Speech]], and her next two projects, ''NadirahSongs'' and ''Obsessed with Peace Vol. I'' were released independently. In 2000, she teamed up with her best friend, world-renowned producer [[Osunlade]]. Together, they released several [[House music|house-music]] songs on Osunlade\u2019s [[Yoruba Records]] label that quickly became classics of the genre. \"Love Song,\" \"Just a Breath Away,\" and \"Pride\" are three of their most popular collaborations.\n\nOn October 14, 2008, Nadirah released a new album titled ''Nod to the Storyteller'' on Jimmy Buffett's Mailboat Records label, which includes two songs written by Ms. Shakoor along with unique covers of songs written by Jimmy Buffett and several other artists. She announced on the \"Time after Island Time\" radio program that she will be releasing a follow-up album. After the release, Nadirah and her brother, drummer Rasheed Shakoor, put together a band called Outside Art to help promote the album and to bring more deep house to the live-music scene.\n\nShe is currently a member of singer & guitarist Jimmy Buffett's band, known as the \"Coral Reefer Band.\" She has done so for almost over two decades. released in 1991. This was the group's biggest commercial success, reaching number 3 in the [[UK Singles Chart]] for three weeks.<ref name=\"British Hit Singles & Albums\">{{cite book\n| first= David\n| last= Roberts\n| year= 2006\n| title= British Hit Singles & Albums\n| edition= 19th\n| publisher= Guinness World Records Limited \n| location= London\n| page= 403\n| isbn= 1-904994-10-5}}</ref>  The track also made the [[Australia]]n [[Top 40|Top 20]]. \n\nLater that year they released the follow-up, \"Wicked Love\", which reached number 25 in the UK [[record chart|singles chart]].<ref>{{cite web|title=Everyhit.com|url=http://www.everyhit.com/}}</ref> In 1992 the act released their first and only [[album]], entitled ''That Compact Disc By Oceanic'', (also, ''That Cassette/LP By Oceanic'' for the [[audio cassette]]/[[Gramophone record|LP]] versions respectively) which featured two different versions of \"Insanity\", and reached a chart position of number 49 before dropping out of the [[UK Albums Chart]] after only 2 weeks. Debuting alongside none other than Tim Bergling, a.k.a. [[Avicii]] and Swedish peer [[Oliver Ingrosso]], with their collaboration \u2018iTrack\u2019. Followed by his breakthrough single \u2018[[Million Voices]]\u2019, created in the back room of the studio whilst Ingrosso and [[Alesso]] penned festival favourite \u2018Calling\u2019. \u2018Million Voices\u2019 would propel the young producer forwards, proving a consistent favorite both across the airwaves and in clubs and setting the benchmark for his productions at an all-time-high. Receiving widespread attention \u2018Million Voices\u2019 crossed over into mainstream consciousness, topping the Shazam chart and being added to the prestigious A playlist at [[BBC Radio 1]], reaching a surge of new fans with each airing. [[record producer|producer]] who formerly went under the moniker '''Club 69''' as well as '''Size Queen'''. A native of [[Vienna]], [[Austria]], he was famous for a variety of his remixes including [[Cher]]'s \"[[Believe (Cher song)|Believe]]\" and a number of [[Madonna (entertainer)|Madonna]]'s [[song]]s including \"[[Nothing Really Matters]]\", \"[[American Life]]\", \"[[Nothing Fails]]\", \"Nobody Knows Me\", \"[[Get Together (Madonna song)|Get Together]]\", \"[[Impressive Instant]]\" and \"[[4 Minutes (Madonna song)|4 Minutes]]\", as well as her collaboration with [[Britney Spears]], \"[[Me Against the Music]]\" and various collaborations with [[Janet Jackson]] (\"[[Throb (song)|Throb]]\" and \"[[Just A Little While]]\" to name a few). He was also behind the [[tribal house]] record label Star 69 and was a frequent producer of the label's releases."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"1692658":{"pageid":1692658,"ns":0,"title":"Phuture","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{Infobox musical artist\n| name                = Phuture\n| background          = group_or_band\n| alias               = Phortune\n| origin              = [[Chicago]], [[USA]]\n| genre               = [[Acid house]], [[deep house]]\n| years_active        = 1985&ndash;present \n| label               = [[Trax Records]]<br>[[Music Man Records]]<br>[[Strictly Rhythm Records]]<br>[[A1 Records]]\n| associated_acts     = [[DJ Pierre]], [[Roy Davis Jr.]]\n| current_members     = [[Earl Smith Jr.|Spanky]]<br>[[Rio]]<br>[[DJ Pierre]]\n| notable_instruments = [[Roland TB-303]]<br>[[Roland TR-707]]\n}}\n\n'''Phuture''' is a [[Chicago]]-based [[Acid house|acid-house]] group founded in 1985 by Spanky, [[DJ Pierre]] and Herb J. The group's 12-minute track \"[[Acid Tracks]]\" (1987) is one of several recordings that lay claim to being the first-ever acid house record.<ref>IMO Records. http://www.imorecords.co.uk/house-2/house-artists/phuture-biography/ \"Phuture Biography\"], ''[[IMO Records]]' Retrieved on 29 March 2011.</ref>\n\n\"Acid Tracks\" featured characteristic bass lines from the [[Roland TB-303]] bass synthesizer\u2014which was manipulated to produce resonant and squelchy sounds uncharacteristic for a bass guitar it was designed to emulate. The track rose to popularity at DJ [[Ron Hardy]]'s [[Music Box (club)|Music Box]] club in Chicago and has since been re-pressed many times.\n\nPhuture released a great number of acid tracks now considered classics, usually as 12-inch [[vinyl record|vinyl]] [[maxi single]]s.\n\nThe music the group produces is dark and monotonous. Many tracks are very long, even passing the 10-minute mark (such as \"Acid Tracks\"). Sparse lyrics are occasionally related to drugs, like the lyrics of \"Your Only Friend\" (1987), which describe [[cocaine]] [[Substance dependence|addiction]], or a simple chant, such as on \"[[Spirit (12-inch single)|Spirit]]\" (1994).\n\nThe group also recorded under several [[pseudonym]]s, generally using the substitution of ph or pf for f. For example, the name Phortune or Pfortune."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"19883265":{"pageid":19883265,"ns":0,"title":"Phuturistix","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{notability|Music|date=April 2015}}\n{{Infobox musical artist <!-- See Wikipedia:WikiProject_Musicians -->\n| name                = Phuturistix\n| image                 = \n| caption            = \n| image_size            = \n| background          = group_or_band\n| alias               = \n| origin              = [[United Kingdom]]\n| genre               = [[UK garage]], [[broken beat]]\n| years_active        = Late 1990s\u2013present\n| label               = [[Locked On Records|Locked On]], [[Hospital Records|Hospital]], Phuture Lounge\n| associated_acts     = \n| website                 = \n| current_members     = [[Zed Bias]] and DJ Injekta\n| past_members        = \n}}\n'''Phuturistix''' is an [[England|English]] musical duo consisting of [[Zed Bias]] (real name Dave Jones) and DJ Injekta (real name Sefton Motley) who operate within the [[UK garage]] and [[broken beat]] genres. When this group formed in 1981 on radio station [[WVAZ|WBMX]], Rosario, the youngest member of the group, was still in high school. The Hot Mix 5 went on to become one of the leading forces in the early Chicago [[house music]] scene.\n\nLike other members of the group, Rosario eventually branched out into music production and remixing. His first release, made in collaboration with Vince Edwards, was \"Sample That!\" in 1986 under the name Bang Orchestra. In 1987, his collaboration with [[Xaviera Gold]], \"[[You Used to Hold Me]]\", became a big hit for Rosario that was subsequently remixed and re-released several times.\n\nRosario continues to work as a DJ and remixer and has released several full-length albums. He has remixed tracks by artists including [[INXS]], [[the Shamen]], [[Jomanda (group)|Jomanda]], [[Culture Beat]], [[Gloria Estefan]], [[Deee-Lite]], [[Pet Shop Boys]], [[Madonna (entertainer)|Madonna]], [[Michael Bubl\u00e9]], [[Mariah Carey]], [[Ricky Martin]], [[Kelly Clarkson]], [[Pussycat Dolls]] and [[Liza Fox]].\n\nOn December 1, 2011, it was announced that Rosario, along with producing partner Abel Aguilera, received a 2012 Grammy nomination for the Rosabel Club Mix of the Rihanna track \"[[Only Girl (In the World)]]\"."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"36303269":{"pageid":36303269,"ns":0,"title":"Raze (house music group)","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"#REDIRECT [[Raze (house-music group)]]"}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"188454":{"pageid":188454,"ns":0,"title":"Real McCoy (band)","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{Other uses|The Real McCoy (disambiguation)}}\n{{Infobox musical artist <!-- See Wikipedia:WikiProject_Musicians -->\n| name                = Real McCoy\n| image               = \n| caption             = \n| image_size          = 250\n| background          = group_or_band\n| alias               = \n| origin              = [[Berlin]], Germany\n| instrument          = \n| genre               = [[pop music|Pop]], [[eurodance]], [[techno]], [[hi-NRG]], [[electronic music|electronic]], [[euro disco]],  [[downtempo]]\n| occupation          = \n| years_active        = 1988\u2013present\n| label               = Phears Music/SME Records<br>Arista/BMG Records\n| associated_acts     = \n| website             = {{URL|http://www.realmccoy.de}}\n| current_members     = [[O-Jay|Olaf Jeglitza]]<br/>Debbie Butts<br/>[[Gemma J|Gemma Sampson]]\n}}\n'''Real McCoy''', originally known as '''M.C. fictional character from the Al-Qadim campaign setting of Dungeons & Dragons, see [[Selan (Dungeons & Dragons)]].''\n\n{{Infobox musical artist <!-- See Wikipedia:WikiProject_Musicians -->\n| name                = Selan\n\n| background          = solo_singer\n| alias               = Selonius, Selonius Funk\n| origin              = [[Queens, New York]], [[U.S.A.]]\n| genre               = [[Contemporary R&B|R&B]], [[House Music|House]], [[Electronica]], [[Soul music|Soul]], [[Rock music|Rock]]\n| years_active        = 2000&ndash;present\n| label               = [[Selonius Records]], [[Vega Records]]\n| associated_acts     = [[The Free Radikalz]], [[Louie Vega]], [[Kenny \"Dope\" Gonzales]], [[DJ Spinna]], [[Alejandro Sanz]], [[Adele]], [[Ashanti (entertainer)|Ashanti]], [[Raheem DeVaughn]], [[Dennis Ferrer]]\n| website                 =\n| current_members     =\n| past_members        =\n| notable_instruments = piano, keyboards, drum programming, trumpet, drums, electric bass\n}}\n\n'''Selan''' (born '''Selan Lerner''' in [[Queens]], [[New York]], [[United States]]) is an American musician, singer, songwriter, composer, arranger, musical director and producer who is known for combining [[electronic music|electronic]], [[pop (music)|pop]], and [[soul music]]. He possesses [[perfect pitch]] and musical total recall, also known as [[eidetic memory]]. He is of [[Trinidadian]] and [[Jewish]] heritage.\n\nSelan has collaborated extensively with [[\"Little\" Louie Vega]] and [[Kenny \"Dope\" Gonzales]] of the house music production team [[Masters at Work]]. Notably he plays the extended keyboard improvisation on the [[Masters at Work]] remix of [[Nina Simone]]'s \"[[See-Line Woman]]\" which appears on the highly successful 2002 [[Verve Remixed]] collection. He also plays the extended keyboard solos on the [[DJ Spinna]] remix of [[Betty Carter]]'s \"Naima's Love Song\" which appears on the 2003 follow-up [[Verve Remixed]] 2 collection. Selan co-wrote the music for most of [[DJ Spinna]]'s Intergalactic Soul album, which was released in 2006 on [[Shanachie]] Records. He also co-produced, co-wrote and was a featured artist on \"Back 2 U\", a standout track on that same album.\n\nHis 2004 single \"Unconditional Love,\" produced by DJ Spinna, was released on the Wonderwax record label. Selan's solo single \"Gravity\" was released in 2005 on Louie Vega's Vega Records. He is the co-writer of the song \"Focus\" which appears on [[Concrete Rose]], the multi-platinum 2004 album by American [[R&B]] singer [[Ashanti (entertainer)|Ashanti]]. He also appears as a co-writer on the songs \"Marathon\" and \"Desire\" which appear on the 2007 [[Grammy]]-nominated second album [[Love Behind the Melody]] by [[Raheem DeVaughn]].\n\nAs a side musician, he has performed with Adele, Alejandro Sanz, Rihanna, Miley Cyrus, R&B singer Joe, Stevie Wonder and Roy Ayers just to name a few. He's recorded with and/or for Kanye West, Aaliyah, David Byrne, Earth, Wind and Fire, R. Kelly, Musiq Soulchild and many others. Selan's keyboard work on the house remix for Curtis Mayfield's \"Superfly\" helped DJ/producer Louie Vega win the 2006 Grammy award for BEST REMIX.  He has been a member of Little Louie Vega's Elements of Life Band and also plays keyboards and sings background for the classic disco/R&B group CHIC featuring Nile Rodgers.\n\nAfter being traveling as part of Adele's band from January 2009-July 2009, Selan joined the classic r&b/disco band, Chic featuring Nile Rodgers. He played keyboards and sang background.\n\nIn September 2011, Selan joined the house band as a keyboardist, vocalist and trumpet player for [[Rosie O'Donnell]]'s \"The Rosie Show\" which aired on [[Oprah Winfrey]]'s OWN network. It was cancelled in March 2012.\n\nOn August 8, 2012 Selan released his debut album, \"Space Flight\", which features contributions from legendary producer/guitarist/songwriter and artist [[Nile Rodgers]], [[Ali Shaheed Muhammad]] of [[A Tribe Called Quest]] fame, [[M-1 (rapper)|M1]] from the revolutionary hip-hop group [[Dead Prez]], Grammy-nominated recording artist [[Emily King]] and Melissa Jimenez.\n\n2013 was a big year for Nile Rodgers, who wound up winning 3 Grammys for his work on Daft Punk's album, \"Random Access Memories\". All of the frenzy surrounding the song \"Get Lucky\" brought a very high visibility to Chic and as well as to Nile himself. The band toured all over the world rejuvenating Nile's career and introducing him to a younger generation. Despite all of this success and exposure, Selan decided to leave the band in January 2014 and subsequently retire from being a side musician period. He decided to focus all of his efforts on music production, his solo career, filmmaking and other business ventures.\n\nHe is currently completing his forthcoming album for a summer 2015 release, developing TV show ideas and short films and also creating vegan clothing and footwear. Selan is vegan and an environmental, human and animal rights activist."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"43944424":{"pageid":43944424,"ns":0,"title":"Shakedown (group)","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"#REDIRECT [[Shakedown (band)]]\n{{R from move}}"}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"1148551":{"pageid":1148551,"ns":0,"title":"The Shamen","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{EngvarB|date=August 2014}}\n{{Use dmy dates|date=August 2014}}\n{{distinguish|Shaman|Shaymen|Samen}}\n{{About|the music group|the album by Pep Love and Jay Biz|Shamen (album)}}\n{{Refimprove|date=August 2009}}\n{{Infobox musical artist <!-- See WP:WikiProject_Musicians -->\n| name                = Shamen\n| image               = Shamen.jpg\n| caption = Mr. C, Victoria Wilson James, Colin Angus (from left to right)\n| image_size          = \n| background          = group_or_band\n| origin              = [[Aberdeen]], [[Scotland]]\n| instrument          = \n| genre               = [[Techno]], [[acid house]], [[alternative dance]], [[rave music|rave]], [[alternative rock]]\n| occupation          = \n| years_active        = 1985\u20131999\n| label               = [[Moksha Records|Moksha]], [[One Little Indian Records]], [[Epic Records|Epic]]\n| associated_acts     = \n| website             =\n| current_members     = \n| past_members        = Colin Angus<br/>Bob Breeks<br/>John Delafons<br/>Gavin Knight<br/>Plavka Lonich<br/>Derek McKenzie<br/>Keith McKenzie<br/>Angus Oakey<br/>Allison Morrison<br/>Richard Sharpe<br/>[[Will Sinnott]]<small>(deceased) </small><br/>Peter Stephenson<br/>[[Mr C|Richard West (Mr C)]]<br/>Victoria Wilson James\n| notable_instruments = \n}}\n\n'''Shamen''' were a Scottish [[psychedelic music|psychedelic]]-influenced [[electronic dance music]] band from [[Aberdeen]], Scotland.  The founding members are Colin Angus (born 24 August 1961), Derek McKenzie (born 27 February 1964) and Keith McKenzie (born 30 August 1961). Peter Stephenson (born 1 March 1962) joined shortly after to take over on keyboards from Angus. Several other people were later in the band. Angus then teamed up with Will Sinnott, and together they found credibility as pioneers of rock/dance crossover. When [[Mr. C]] joined, the band moved on to international commercial success with \"[[Ebeneezer Goode]]\" and their 1992 ''[[Boss Drum]]'' album."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"33011084":{"pageid":33011084,"ns":0,"title":"Shapeshifters (band)","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"#REDIRECT [[The Shapeshifters]]"}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"2180381":{"pageid":2180381,"ns":0,"title":"Shawn Christopher","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{distinguish|Shawn Chrystopher (rapper)}}\n{{BLP sources|date=March 2008}}\n'''Shawn Christopher''' is a female [[African-American]] [[House music|house-music]] [[singing|singer]] from [[Chicago]], [[Illinois]]."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"866746":{"pageid":866746,"ns":0,"title":"Shep Pettibone","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{rewrite|date=April 2014}}\n{{Infobox musical artist <!-- See Wikipedia:WikiProject_Musicians -->\n| name                = Shep Pettibone\n| caption            = \n| image_size            = \n| background          = non_performing_personnel\n| birth_name          = \n| alias               = \n| birth_date                =  \n|birth_place ={{flagicon|US}} [[United States]]\n| origin              = \n| instrument          = \n| genre               = [[Dance-pop]]<br/>[[Post-disco]]<br/>[[House music|House]]<br/>[[Electronic dance music|Club]]\n| occupation          = [[Disk jockey|DJ]], [[Music producer]], [[Remix]]er\n| years_active        = 1980s\u2013present\n| label               = \n| associated_acts     = [[Madonna (entertainer)|Madonna]], [[Janet Jackson]], Tony Humphries\n| website                 = \n| current_members     = \n| past_members        = \n| notable_instruments = \n}}\n\n'''Shep Pettibone''' is a [[record producer]], remixer, songwriter and club [[Disc jockey|DJ]], one of the most prolific of the 1980s. His earliest work known to the public was for one of New York City's top urban radio station, [[WEPN-FM|WRKS 98.7 Kiss-FM]], and later as remixer/producer for the [[disco]]/[[dance music|dance]] label [[Salsoul Records]]. His prowess at production and mixing led him to work with such artists as [[Madonna (entertainer)|Madonna]] and [[George Michael]] in the late 1980s during the height of these artists' popularity. Together with [[Arthur Baker (musician)|Arthur Baker]], he helped to popularize many aspects of dance and hip-hop culture, such as [[scratching]].<ref>http://www.allmusic.com/artist/shep-pettibone-p114035</ref>\n<!-- Unsourced image removed: [[Image:shep2.gif]] -->\n\nSince 1998, Pettibone has owned the Paradise Nightclub and [[The Empress Hotel (New Jersey)|the Empress Hotel]] in [[Asbury Park, New Jersey]].<ref>[http://web.archive.org/web/20040625153652/http://www.gayasburypark.com/more.tpl?w=3294077241 \"Empress Hotel Renovations Moving Quickly.\"] ''Gay Asbury Park''. 14 May 2004.</ref>"}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"24597172":{"pageid":24597172,"ns":0,"title":"Showtek","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{Infobox musical artist <!-- See Wikipedia:WikiProject Musicians -->\n| name = Showtek\n| image = showtek.jpg\n| caption =\n| image_size =\n| background = group_or_band\n| origin = [[Eindhoven]], [[The Netherlands]]\n| instrument =\n| genre = [[Techno]] <small>(2001\u20132003)</small><br />[[Hardstyle]] <small>(2003\u20132012)</small><br />[[Electronic dance music|EDM]], [[progressive house]], [[electro house]] <small>(2012\u2013present)</small>\n| occupation = Producers\n| years_active = 2001\u2013present\n| label = Musical Freedom, [[OWSLA]] , [[Revealed Recordings]], [[Spinnin' Records]], Skink Records.\n| associated_acts = Tiesto, Hardwell, Justin Prime, Bassjackers, Noisecontrollers, We are Loud!, [[Sonny Wilson]], David Guetta, Ookay, [[Vassy (singer)|Vassy]], [[Elliphant]], [[Ms Dynamite]], [[Martin Garrix]].\n| website = http://www.showtek.nl\n| current_members = Wouter Janssen<br> Sjoerd Janssen\n}}\n\n'''Showtek''' is a Dutch [[electronic dance music]] act consisting of two brothers, Sjoerd Janssen (born 1984) and Wouter Janssen (born 1982), who began producing music in 2001. Starting out with techno and subsequently moving to [[hardstyle]], they eventually worked in other EDM styles including progressive/electro house. In 2012, the Showtek brothers began a series of collaborations, a project called Crazy Collabs, with producers from some of the other genres in dance music. Before the official announcement of their collaboration, they co-produced an EP with [[Ti\u00ebsto]] and [[Angger Dimas]] entitled \"We Rock\" as Boys Will Be Boys. On their project, they have worked with Ti\u00ebsto, Hardwell, Justin Prime, Bassjackers, Ookay, [[MAKJ]] and hardstyle duo Noisecontrollers. \"Baldy & Cresty\" are the cartoon [[alter ego]]s of the two brothers. Showtek also co-produced the upcoming single of [[Chris Brown (American entertainer)|Chris Brown]] \u2013 ''Nobody's Perfect'' which is produced by [[Lukas Hilbert]] and co-produced by Showtek and David Jost.{{citation needed|date=December 2013}}  The Showtek brothers also have their own podcast, available through their website and iTunes. In December 2013, they founded their own label Skink Records, which is a sub-label of Spinnin' Records.\n\nThe duo recently founded their own label \"Skink Records\", which is licensed to [[Spinnin Records]] but is however not a sublabel of [[Spinnin Records|Spinnin]]. Growing up in [[Northeast Los Angeles]] and in [[Northern California]], Sonny Moore joined the American [[post-hardcore]] band [[From First to Last]] as the [[Lead vocalist|lead singer]] in 2004, and recorded two [[studio album]]s with the band (''[[Dear Diary, My Teen Angst Has a Body Count]]'', 2004, and ''[[Heroine (From First to Last album)|Heroine]]'', 2006) before leaving to pursue a solo career in 2007.<ref name=RTTNews>{{cite news |title= Korn Preview New Track 'Get Up' |url= http://www.rttnews.com/Content/EntertainmentNews.aspx?Section=2&Id=1600207&SM=1 |work=RTT News |date=April 18, 2011 |accessdate=April 26, 2011}}</ref><ref name=\"Brand X\">{{cite news |last= Siegal |first= Daniel |title=Coachella 2011: Our body-grooving guide to the dance tents |url= http://thisisbrandx.com/2011/04/coachella-2011-our-body-grooving-guide-to-the-dance-tents/ |work=Brand X|work=Los Angeles Times|accessdate=April 26, 2011}}</ref> He began his first tour as a solo artist in late 2007. After recruiting a new band lineup, Moore joined the [[Alternative Press Tour]] to support bands such as [[All Time Low]] and [[The Rocket Summer]], and appeared on the cover of ''[[Alternative Press|Alternative Press']]'' annual \"100 Bands You Need to Know\" issue.<ref name=top100>{{cite web |title=100 Bands You Need to Know |url= http://www.altpress.com/magazine/issue/237-1_-_100_bands_you_need_to_know_2008/ |work= Alternative Press |year=2008 |accessdate=April 21, 2011}}</ref>\n\nAfter releasing the ''[[Gypsyhook EP|Gypsyhook]]'' [[Extended play|EP]] in 2009, Moore was scheduled to record his debut studio album, ''Bells'', with producer Noah Shain. However, he ceased production of the album and began performing under the name Skrillex, distributing the ''[[My Name Is Skrillex]]'' EP for free [[Music download|download]] on his official [[MySpace]] page. Subsequently, he released the ''[[Scary Monsters and Nice Sprites]]'' EP in late\u20132010 and ''[[More Monsters and Sprites]]'' EP in mid\u20132011, both of which have since become moderate commercial successes. On November 30, 2011, he was nominated for a total of five [[Grammy Award]]s at the [[54th Grammy Awards]], including [[Grammy Award for Best New Artist|Best New Artist]] and won three: \"Best Dance/Electronica Album\", \"Best Dance Recording\", and \"Best Remixed Recording, Non-Classical\".<ref name=\"Grammys\">{{cite web|title=Nominees And Winners |url= http://www.grammy.com/nominees |accessdate=November 30, 2011}}</ref> On December 5, 2011, the [[BBC]] announced that he had been nominated for their [[Sound of...|Sound of 2012]] poll.<ref>{{cite web| url= http://www.bbc.co.uk/music/soundof/2012/artists/skrillex/ |title=Sound of \u2013 2012 \u2013 Skrillex |publisher=BBC |accessdate=2012-02-14}}</ref> On December 12, 2011, he was also named [[MTV]]'s [[Electronic dance music|Electronic Dance Music]] Artist of the Year.<ref>{{cite news |url= http://www.mtv.com/news/articles/1675816/skrillex-best-edm-artist-2011.jhtml \n|title= Skrillex Is MTV's EDM Artist Of 2011! |work=MTV |date=December 12, 2011 |accessdate=2012-02-14}}</ref> Skrillex has won a total of six [[Grammy Award]]s. The Wailers approached producer [[Lee \"Scratch\" Perry]] in August 1970 to record an entire album, and the sessions took place at [[Randy's Recording Studio|Randy's Studio 17]] in [[Kingston, Jamaica]], until November. First issued in the UK by [[Trojan Records]] in December 1970, the album has since been re-released several times on several different labels. Perry's production is sparse and haunting, only featuring guitar, bass, drums, electronic organs, and vocals with no horns or other embellishments."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"3964553":{"pageid":3964553,"ns":0,"title":"Spiller","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{Other people|Spiller|Spiller (surname)}}\n{{Infobox musical artist <!-- See Wikipedia:WikiProject_Musicians -->\n| name = Spiller\n| image = \n| caption = \n| image_size = \n| background = group_or_band\n| alias               =\n| birth_name = Cristiano Spiller \n| birth_date = {{Birth date and age|1975|4|3|df=y}}\n| origin = [[Venice]], [[Italy]]\n| genre = [[Electronica]], [[House music|house]], [[disco house]]\n| years_active = 1997&ndash;present\n| label = [[EMI]], [[Positiva Records]], [[Nano Records]]\n| associated_acts = \n| website = \n| current_members = \n| past_members = \n| notable_instruments = \n}}\n'''Cristiano Spiller''' (born 3 April 1975) is an [[Italian people|Italian]] [[electronic music]] [[Disc jockey|DJ]]. He began working on the Detroit techno scene in 1990, studying with [[Derrick May (musician)|Derrick May]] and working with him on business ventures. He used the aliases '''Bango, Kosmik Messenger, X-Stacy''' and '''Silent Phase'''. Pullen's incorporation of [[house music|house]] and [[garage house|garage]] with techno has been cited as an influence on later electronic artists.<ref>[{{Allmusic|class=artist|id=p182870/biography|pure_url=yes}} Stacey Pullen] at [[Allmusic]]</ref>"}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"21578035":{"pageid":21578035,"ns":0,"title":"Star Tattooed","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"'''Star Tattooed''' is an indie [[vocal house]] music project by popular Bulgarian award winning songwriter and producer [[Miro Gechev]] and Dary Oreshkova featured on many compilation CDs released in Europe, Russia, and Israel, including the likes of [[David Guetta]], [[Bob Sinclar]], [[Fedde Le Grand]], [[Pakito]] and [[Benny Benassi]]. The project started in the summer of 2005 for a pilot project for Miro's label and recording studio 2AM. The pilot, a song called \"''Make Me High''\" featuring vocals of Ava, became licensed by [[Airplay Records]]/[[Universal Music]] - France, reaching number 30 of the official single sales charts of France. It remained in the French Top 100 Single Sales for 11 weeks.<ref>[http://www.yacast.fr/fr/index.html http://www.yacast.fr/fr/index.html] - Yacast.fr</ref> \"''Make Me High''\" was also awarded the viewers choice for 'best hit' on the 9th annual music awards of Bulgarian music TV channel MMTV. The song entered in the annual Top 100 of Evropa Plus radio (Russia). The videoclip of \"Make Me High\" is directed by Valeri Milev. Single remixed by Enzo Mori & Stephan Clark. \n\nIn 2008, another track by Star Tattooed was released through Airplay Records/Universal Music - France, called \"''What A Music!''\", which reached the top 10 for vinyl sales chart on French ''DJBuzz.com''. The videoclip of \"What A Music!\" is directed by Lachezar Avramov. Single was being remixed by Enzo Mori & Stephan Clark (2007), Fred De F (2008)\n\nIn September 2008, Star Tattooed premiered \"''Wanna See U''\", featuring Bulgarian [[Music Idol]] finalist Plamen, during the 10th annual music awards of MMTV, a Bulgarian music channel. In January 2009, \"''Wanna See U''\" was released digitally while another track was premiered, \"''Baby (What About)''\" featuring Alexandra Raeva, a popular Bulgarian public figure and owner of a commercial clothing brand named Aggata. Silk]]. Edelson, Ph.D.}}</ref> It is considered a way in which people with autism calm and stimulate themselves.<ref name=\"Foley\"/> Therapists view this behavior  as a protective response to being overly sensitive to [[Stimulus (physiology)|stimuli]], with which the individual blocks less predictable environmental stimuli.<ref name=\"Cowell\">{{cite book | url=http://books.google.mk/books?id=JiBo8JYaBjIC&dq=&source=gbs_navlinks_s | title=Help for the Child with Asperger's Syndrome: A Parent's Guide to Negotiating the Social Service Maze | publisher=[[Jessica Kingsley Publishers]] | author=Gretchen Mertz Cowell | year=2004 | isbn=9781846420429}}</ref> [[Sensory processing disorder]] is also given as a reason by some therapists for the condition.<ref name=\"Cowell\"/> Another theory is that stimming is a way to relieve [[anxiety]], and other emotions.<ref>{{cite web | url=http://www.healthcentral.com/autism/c/1443/141549/spectrum-disorders | title=Autism Spectrum Disorders and Anxiety | publisher=[[Health Central]] | date=July 15, 2011 | accessdate=25 March 2014 | author=Eileen Bailey}}</ref>\n\nCommon stimming behaviors (sometimes called ''stims''<ref>{{cite web | url=http://autismdigest.com/why-do-kids-with-autism-stim/ | title=Why Do Kids with Autism Stim? | publisher=Autism Digest | date=November\u2013December 2011 | accessdate=25 March 2014 | author=Temple Grandin, PhD}}</ref>) include: hand flapping, rocking, head banging, repeating noises or words, snapping fingers, spinning objects, etc.<ref name=\"Stimming\">{{cite web | url=http://www.healthcentral.com/autism/c/1443/155585/stimming/ | title=Stimming | publisher=[[Health Central]] | date=August 27, 2012 | accessdate=25 March 2014 | author=Eileen Bailey}}</ref><ref>{{cite web | url=http://www.bbc.com/news/blogs-ouch-22771894 | title=Stimming: What autistic people do to feel calmer | publisher=[[BBC]] | date=5 June 2013 | accessdate=25 March 2014}}</ref> Stimming is almost always a symptom of [[autism]], but it is also regarded as part of some non-autistic individuals' behavioral patterns.<ref name=\"About\">{{cite web | url=http://autism.about.com/od/autismterms/f/stimming.htm | title=Stimming | publisher=[[About.com]] | date=October 13, 2009 | accessdate=24 March 2014 | author=Lisa Jo Rudy}}</ref> The biggest difference between autistic and non-autistic stimming is the type of stim and the quantity of stimming.<ref name=\"About\"/>\n\nIn the [[Diagnostic and Statistical Manual of Mental Disorders]], published by the [[American Psychiatric Association]], this type of behavior is listed as one of the symptoms of autism or a \"stereotyped and repetitive motor mannerisms\".<ref>\u201cAutism Spectrum Disorders,\u201d 1994, Diagnostic and Statistical Manual, American Psychiatric Association</ref> There are numerous ways to reduce or eliminate [[stereotypic behavior]]s.<ref name=\"Stephen\"/> Some of them include providing an individual with alternative forms of stimulation; drugs have been used to reduce stimming (however, it is not clear whether the drugs are actually beneficial or restrict the individual from finding relief).<ref name=\"Stephen\"/>\n\nStimming can, in some cases, be a [[self-injury|self-injurious]] behavior.<ref His single, \u201c[[Electrica Salsa]]\u201d under the alias OFF launched his career in 1986. Lovingly referred to as \u201cPapa Sven\u201d by his fans,<ref name=IMS2013 /> Sven V\u00e4th has made his mark in the music community by being one of Germany\u2019s \u201cpop stars\u201d in the nineties,<ref name=Groove /> running two famous night clubs in Germany, and starting his own company Cocoon, which encompasses a [[booking agency]], [[record label]], and a branch for events. He is recognized for cultivating the underground electronic music scene not just in Germany but in Ibiza as well,<ref name=Groove /> with his own night at Amnesia for fourteen years and after-parties at creative locations around the island. Sven V\u00e4th is a major proponent of vinyl, using only two [[phonograph|decks]] and a mixer for his extensive [[DJ mix|DJ sets]], his longest set having been 30 hours.<ref name=IMS2013 />"}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"3705525":{"pageid":3705525,"ns":0,"title":"Swayzak","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{Infobox musical artist <!-- See Wikipedia:WikiProject_Musicians -->\n| name                = Swayzak\n| image                 = Swayzak.jpg\n| caption            = \n| image_size            = \n| background          = group_or_band\n| alias               = \n| origin              = [[London, England]]\n| genre               = [[Minimal music|Minimal]], [[House music|House]]\n| years_active        = 1993&ndash;present\n| label               = [[!K7 Records|!K7]]<br>[[Fabric]]<br>[[Medicine]]<br>[[Pagan]]<br>[[Swayzak Recordings]]\n| associated_acts     = \n| website                 = \n| current_members     = David Brown\n| past_members        = James S. Taylor\n| notable_instruments = \n}}\n\n'''Swayzak''' is a [[tech house]] duo from the United Kingdom that consists of James S. Taylor and David Brown. They live and work in [[London]] and released their first 12\" single \"Bueno\" / \"Fukumachi\" in February 1997 to much acclaim. It was followed up by the 12\" \"Speedboat\" / \"Low Rez Skyline\" to become part of the burgeoning tech-house scene in the [[United Kingdom|UK]].\n\nTheir debut long player, ''[[Snowboarding in Argentina]]'' was released by [[The Medicine Label]] ([[USA]]) and [[Pagan Records]] ([[United Kingdom|UK]]) in May 1998. It garnered many positive reviews. The album was later chosen as 1998 Album Of The Year in the U.S. dance publication ''[[Mixer (magazine)|Mixer]]''. They went on to release 4 further studio albums making their place in the electronic music canon.\n\nJames Taylor left the group in 2011 to focus on his solo project Lugano Fell. In late 1987, she scored her first major hit when her debut single \"[[Tell It to My Heart]]\" reached No. 7 on the Hot 100. She then went on to have a string of hits in the late 1980s and early 1990s, including the No. 1 ''[[Billboard Hot 100|Billboard]]'' hit \"[[Love Will Lead You Back]]\". Overall, she has had eighteen individual hit songs reach the top ten in ''Billboard'' magazine. These include most recently, the 2011 American and international hit \"Floor on Fire\" and the 2008 song \"[[Beautiful (Taylor Dayne song)|Beautiful]]\", which reached the top spot on the ''[[Billboard (magazine)|Billboard]]'' [[Hot Dance Club Play]] chart. Some of their best-known songs are \"[[Start the Commotion]]\" and \"Ooh La La\" (not to be confused with the [[Goldfrapp]] song of the same name), which were used in commercials for [[Mitsubishi]] and [[Budweiser (Anheuser-Busch)|Budweiser]]. Keating's current project is a duo called [[The Black Ghosts]] where he performs with [[Simon William Lord]], formerly a founding member of rock band [[Simian (band)|Simian]].\n\nKeating is also a popular house and electro DJ and producer, under the name Fake Blood. He has released several successful productions and remixes as Fake Blood, including his 2009 release \"[[I Think I Like It]]\". In 2009, Fake Blood featured on an episode of BBC Radio 1's [[Essential Mix]].<ref>http://www.mixesdb.com/w/2009-03-14_-_Fake_Blood_-_Essential_Mix</ref> \n\nIn May 2012, Fake Blood announced plans in his Facebook for a new 3-track EP, later in 2012, also he's working on the album, that would be released after EP. Later, in July 2012, he stated, that album \"Cells\" would be released this autumn. Burns with Theo Parrish, Tue, 29 Apr 2008</ref> He was born in Washington, DC. He grew up in Chicago, Illinois listening to jazz musicians like Miles Davis, Nina Simone, and George Gershwin.<ref>IMO Records. [http://www.imorecords.co.uk/house-2/house-artists/theo-parrish-biography/ \u201cTheo Parrish Biography\"], ''[[IMO Records]]. Retrieved on 17 April 2011.</ref> He graduated from the Chicago Academy of the Arts and went to study at the [[Kansas City Art Institute]]. While at KCAI, he concentrated on sound sculptures, creating sonic pieces by combining live instruments, human voices, and looped recordings. He received his BFA in 1994 and moved to Michigan to focus on musical projects.<ref>[http://www.inthemix.com.au/features/45249/Theo_Parrish_Sound_sculptor In the Mix Features Theo Parrish ] interview by JadeJade 15 Dec 2009</ref>\n\nHe has recorded music under his own name as well as with [[Rick Wilhite]], [[Marcellus Malik Pittman]] and [[Moodymann|Kenneth Dixon Jr]] as [[3 Chairs]].<ref>[http://www.thestranger.com/seattle/data-breaker/Content?oid=25424 The Stranger ] review by Dave Segal 1 Dec 2005</ref> He also puts out releases on his record label, Sound Signature. Another aspect of Theo Parrish's productions are his re-edits, often of old disco, funk or soul records. He is almost as renowned for his expansive and genre-hopping live DJ sets as his productions, and plays a monthly residency at the London nightclub Plastic People."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"33040297":{"pageid":33040297,"ns":0,"title":"The Third Twin (duo)","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{Orphan|date=April 2012}}\n{{Infobox musical artist  \n| Name                = The Third Twin\n| Background          = group_or_band\n| Alias               = Le Troisi\u00e8me Jumeau\n| Origin              = {{Flag | France}}, Paris\n| Genre               =  [[Electronic dance music|EDM]], [[electronica]], [[Trance (music genre)|trance]], [[progressive house]], [[electro house]], [[dubstep]]\n| Occupation          =  [[Record producer|Producers]]\n| Years_active        = 2010 - 2011\n| Label               = [[Crydaroul\u00e9]] (2010 - 2011)\n| Former_members      = Yvan de Homem Christo <br> Virgille de Homem Christo\n}}\n'''The Third Twin''' is a [[French house]] musical duo made up by the twin brothers Yvan and Virgille de Homem-Christo, who are said to be nephews of [[Guy-Manuel de Homem-Christo]], of [[Daft Punk]].<ref name=\"Interview @ Noctamina (Spanish Blog)\">\"The Third Twin: los entrevistamos para zanjar pol\u00e9micas\" ''Noctamina''. 24 March 2011. http://www.noctamina.com/entrevistas/the-third-twin-los-entrevistamos-para-zanjar-polemicas.</ref> The duo claim to be a philosophical-musical project that is aimed at progressing human development into a global society.<ref name=\"philosophical-musical project\">Tempia, Simone. \"The Third Twin: Exclusive interview with the mysterious duo that is said to be Daft Punk.\" ''Vogue Italia''. 15 January 2011. Harris had previously worked as part of several music groups including [[Kon Kan]], Top Kat, [[Killer Bunnies (dance project)|Killer Bunnies and Outta Control]] and had also released several solo singles himself.  Cox, a musician and DJ, had also worked for years as a DJ and producer, producing a [[remix|megamix]] of [[Paula Abdul]] songs, among other things, and started his own record label, Interhit Records, with Jeff Johnson."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"1609544":{"pageid":1609544,"ns":0,"title":"Tiefschwarz","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{refimprove|date=May 2013}}\n\n{{Infobox musical artist  <!-- See Wikipedia:WikiProject Musicians -->\n| name                = Tiefschwarz\n| image                 = Tiefschwarz @ Venue.jpg\n| caption            = \n| image_size            = \n| background          = group_or_band\n| origin              = [[Stuttgart]], [[Germany]]\n| genre               = [[House music|House]], [[Tech House]], [[Electro music|Electro]]\n| years_active        = 1996&ndash;\n| label               = \n| associated_acts     = \n| website                 = http://www.tiefschwarz.net\n| current_members     = Alexander Schwarz<br />Sebastian Schwarz\n| past_members        =  Peter Hoff\n| notable_instruments = \n}}\n\n'''Tiefschwarz''' is a [[tech house]] group comprising brothers, Alexander \"Ali\" (June 7, 1967-) and Sebastian \"Basti\" (December 28, 1969-) Schwarz, which formed in [[Stuttgart]] in 1996.<ref>IMO Records. [http://www.imorecords.co.uk/house-2/house-artists/tiefschwarz-biography/ \"Tiefschwarz Biography\"], ''[[IMO Records]]. Retrieved on 17 April 2011.</ref> Peter Hoff, who runs the Benztown studios in Stuttgart, joined later, and completed the first Tiefschwarz production team. Their name means \"deep black\" in German, and is a combination of the brothers' surnames, and their love of deep house.\n\nTheir earliest productions were released on the Continuemusics label in 1997, and their first taste of a well-respected label was with their ''Music'' track on [[Fran\u00e7ois Kevorkian]]'s [[Wave Music]] label in 1999. The team released their first album, ''RAL9005'' on the [[Four Music]] label in 2001, which was later licensed to [[Derrick Carter]] and [[Luke Solomon]]'s [[Classic Recordings]] label. Tiefschwarz continued to release on Classic until its collapse in 2005, as well as releasing on labels such as Fine and [[International DeeJay Gigolo Records]].\nMany of their tracks have been licensed to compilations, from the [[Stereo Sushi]] series, to compilations for [[Bugged Out!]], [[Get Physical]] and [[Renaissance (club)|Renaissance]], and in 2006, they released [[Fabric 29|a mix of their own]] for the [[Fabric (club)|Fabric]] (London) [[Fabric mix albums|mix series]].\n\nTheir sound is considered, at least by those who have followed them from their Classic days, to have changed somewhat over the last few years. Instead of their original deep, mellow house, Tiefschwarz now represent a gritty and edgy electro house sound, their more recent tracks gaining recognition from the likes of [[Ivan Smagghe]], Touch\u00e9, [[Sasha (DJ)|Sasha]] and [[Danny Howells]].\n\nAli and Basti Schwarz have been travelling Europe as DJs since 1995, playing at major events and popular clubs all over Germany and Switzerland, as well as making appearances in Ibiza.  They've performed in cities as far afield as Miami, New York, Melbourne, Sydney, Amsterdam, Sarajevo, London, Antwerp and Stockholm.\n\nTiefschwarz have composed remixes for [[Madonna (entertainer)|Madonna]]'s ''[[Get Together (Madonna song)|Get Together]]'', [[Missy Elliott]]'s ''[[Teary Eyed]]'' and [[Depeche Mode]]'s single, ''[[John the Revelator / Lilian|John the Revelator]]''.\n\n2007 sees a return to a deeper house sound as shown in their 10 years anniversary compilation; ''10 Years Of Blackmusik''.\n\nIn January and July 2011 Tiefschwarz performed at the legendary aftershow party of the [[StyleNite]], a cultural event of the designer [[Michael Michalsky]] during Berlin Fashion Week."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"316044":{"pageid":316044,"ns":0,"title":"The Timelords","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"#redirect [[Time Lord]]"}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"892372":{"pageid":892372,"ns":0,"title":"Ti\u00ebsto","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{Infobox musical artist <!-- See Wikipedia:WikiProject_Musicians -->\n|name = Ti\u00ebsto\n|image = DJ Ti\u00ebsto.jpg\n|caption =\n|image_size = 240px\n|landscape = yes\n|background = non_vocal_instrumentalist\n|birth_name = Tijs Michiel Verwest\n|alias = Allure (until 2011), Steve Forte Rio, Da Joker, DJ Limited, DJ Ti\u00ebsto, Drumfire, Handover Circuit, Boys Will Be Boys, Passenger, Roze, Stray Dog, Tom Ace, TST, Wild Bunch<ref name=\"discogs.com\">{{cite web|url=http://www.discogs.com/artist/447026-Tijs-Verwest |title=Tijs Verwest Discography at Discogs |publisher=Discogs.com |date=1969-01-17 |accessdate=2014-04-27}}</ref>\n|birth_date = {{birth date and age|df=yes|1969|1|17}}\n|birth_place = [[Breda]], [[Netherlands]]<ref>[http://www.tiesto.com/Tiesto-professional-life ARTIST]. Ti\u00ebsto met producer Dennis Waakop Reijers in 1998, and the two have worked together extensively since then.<ref name=\"DJ Times - Dennis Waakop Reijers\">{{cite news |last=Tan |first=Emily |title=Ti\u00ebsto Returns With \"Elements of Life,\" Another Crowd-Pleasing Dish of Melodic Trance. His 2000 remix of [[Delerium]]'s \"[[Silence (song)|Silence]]\" featuring [[Sarah McLachlan]] exposed him to more mainstream audiences. In 2001, he released his first solo album, ''[[In My Memory]]. '' The title track is a remix of an original song written by and featuring [[Nicola Hitchcock]]. This album gave him several major hits that launched his career. He was voted World No 1 DJ by [[DJ Magazine]] in its annual Top 100 DJs readership poll consecutively for three years from 2002 to 2004.\n\nJust after releasing his second studio album ''[[Just Be]]'' he performed live at the [[2004 Summer Olympics opening ceremony]] in [[Athens]], the first DJ to play live on stage at an Olympics. In April 2007 Ti\u00ebsto launched his radio show ''[[Ti\u00ebsto's Club Life]]'' on [[Radio 538]] in the Netherlands and released his third studio album ''[[Elements of Life]]''. nomination\">{{cite news |title=50th Annual Grammy Awards Nominations |url=http://www.variety.com/awardcentral_article/VR1117977172.html?nav=news&categoryid=1983&cs=1 |publisher=Variety Award for Best Remixed Recording, Non-Classical]] for his remixed version of [[John Legend|John Legend's]] Top 40 Hit ''[[All of Me (John Legend song)|All Of Me]]'' at the [[57th Annual Grammy Awards]]."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"1701874":{"pageid":1701874,"ns":0,"title":"Tiga (musician)","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{distinguish2|the American Montreal, Canada) is a Canadian musician, [[DJ]] and record producer of [[electronic dance music]]. Tiga {{IPAc-en|\u02c8|t|i\u02d0|\u0261|\u0259}} has released two albums entitled ''[[Sexor]]'' and ''[[Ciao! (Tiga album)|Ciao!]]'' ''Sexor'' won the [[Juno Awards of 2007|2007 Juno Award]] for Dance Recording of the Year. Tiga released a selection of compilations in the early 2000s, featuring mixes such as ''American Gigolo'', ''[[DJ-Kicks: Tiga]]'' and, ''Mixed Emotions'', which put him on the map as one of \"the world's best mixers\".<ref>http://www.allmusic.com/album/mixed-emotions-montreal-mix-sessions-vol-5-mw0000117625</ref> His most recent compilation mix, ''Tiga Non-Stop'', was released in November 2012, and premiered Tiga's latest single \"Plush.\"<ref>http://www.residentadvisor.net/review-view.aspx?id=11960</ref> The mix also features tracks from artists such as [[Kindness (musician)|Kindness]], [[Duke Dumont]] and Blawan.\n\nTiga has remixed songs from the likes of [[The xx]], [[LCD Soundsystem]], [[The Kills]], [[Cabaret Voltaire (band)|Cabaret Voltaire]], [[Scissor Sisters]], [[Peaches (musician)|Peaches]], [[Moby]], [[Depeche Mode]], [[Justice (band)|Justice]], [[Friendly Fires]] and [[Mylo]]. Along with [[Zombie Nation (band)|Zombie Nation]], Tiga is half of [[ZZT (duo)|ZZT]], and has released material as The Dove, Rainer Werner Bassfinder (with Jesper Dahlb\u00e4ck), and TGV (with Mateo Murphy). He has also co-produced music with the likes of [[Soulwax]], [[James Murphy (electronic musician)|James Murphy]], [[Chilly Gonzales]], Jesper Dahlb\u00e4ck, and most recently [[Matthew Dear]], who he worked with on \"Plush.\"\n\nAs a solo artist, Tiga released \"Sunglasses at Night\" with Finnish producer [[Jori Hulkkonen]] (aka Zyntherius). The single reached number 25 in the UK Dance Chart. Other successful chart singles include \"Pleasure From the Bass\", \"You Gonna Want Me\" featuring [[Jake Shears]], and his 2009 release \u201cShoes,\u201d co-produced with Soulwax and Chilly Gonzales.\n\nTiga is the host of the BBC Radio 6 Music show \"My Name Is Tiga\", and made his acting debut in the 2010 film ''[[Ivory Tower (2010 film)|Ivory Tower]]'', co-starring [[Chilly Gonzales]], [[Feist (singer)|Feist]] and [[Peaches (musician)|Peaches]]. The film won special mention at the [[Locarno International Film Festival]]."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"24112248":{"pageid":24112248,"ns":0,"title":"Timmy {{Death date and age|df=yes|YYYY|MM|DD|YYYY|MM|DD}} (death date then birth) -->\n| death_place         = \n| origin              =Sydney\n| instrument          =Trumpet, digital trumpet\n| genre [[Central Station]], Neon Underground, Hussle Recordings\n| associated_acts     =\n| website             = {{Official website|www.timmytrumpet.com}}\n| notable_instruments = Baritone\n}}\n\n'''Timothy Jude Smith'''<ref>http://www.australian-charts.com/showitem.asp?interpret=Timmy+Trumpet+%26+Savage&titel=Freaks&cat=s</ref> (a.k.a. '''Timmy Trumpet''') is a musician, main room [[house music|house]] DJ and producer based in Sydney. Smith made his big break in [[Ibiza]]; playing live trumpet solos over [[electronic dance music]] tracks during DJs shows.\n\nHe has supported and played alongside acts like [[Armin Van Buuren]], [[Carl Cox]], [[Fedde le Grand]], [[Dizzee Rascal]], [[Fatboy Slim]] and the [[Stafford Brothers]].<ref name=\"two\"/> Timmy is also a regular character on the [[FOX8]] reality TV show ''[[The Stafford Brothers]]''.<ref name=\"three\"/>\n\nTimmy Trumpet has successfully transitioned from the international stage as an acclaimed Jazz musician to the realm of global dance music. Now as a combined DJ/Instrumentalist, he's ranked in the top 3 DJ's in Australia (ITM Poll), performed at Ibiza's Pacha and Miami's WMC, and mixed both Ministry of Sound and Pacha CD's. Signed to Ministry of Sound, his last 3 singles have all reached the No. 1 spot on the Aria Club chart. James]] (with whom he shares the same birthdate), co-producing \"En-Trance To Exit\" on the ''[[Analogue Bubblebath]]'' EP for Exeter's influential [[Mighty Force Records]].<ref name=\"Bonacich\">Bonacich, Drago \"[http://www.allmusic.com/artist/tom-middleton-p309903/biography Tom Middleton Biography]\", [[Allmusic]], retrieved 2011-01-22</ref> This was followed by his first solo outing, \"My Splendid Idea\", under the name '''Schizophrenia''' for the same label.\n\nSoon after, he teamed up with [[Mark Pritchard (music producer)|Mark Pritchard]].<ref name=\"Bonacich\" /> The pair recorded under a host of pseudonyms, including the popular [[Reload (band)|Reload]] (featuring experimental [[techno]] and [[ambient music]]), [[Global Communication]] (primarily ambient), and Jedi Knights ([[electro (music)|electro funk]] and [[house music]]), plus lesser-known aliases Chameleon, Secret Ingredients, and Link & E621.<ref name=\"Bonacich\" /> Global Communication's 1994 ambient album ''[[76:14]]'' is widely considered to be a landmark of the genre.<ref name=\"Bonacich\" />\n\nThe pair also founded their own record label, Evolution,<ref name=\"Bonacich\" /> which is sometimes informally referenced as Evolution (Crewekerne) to differentiate it from other record labels with the same name. A compilation of early Evolution material was released jointly by Evolution and [[Warp Records]] in 1995 as ''The Theory of Evolution''. The label name later changed to Universal Language Productions and launched a sublabel, Heard, then became E3 before finally winding down operations. The labels launched early releases from artists such as [[Matthew Herbert]], as well as Middleton & Pritchard under their various guises.\n\nAside from Schizophrenia, Tom's solo projects include '''The Modwheel''' (experimental house music), '''Cosmos''' (progressive house music)<ref name=\"British Hit Singles & Albums\">{{cite book\n| first= David\n| last= Roberts\n| year= 2006\n| title= British Hit Singles & Albums\n| edition= 19th\n| publisher= Guinness World Records Limited \n| location= London\n| isbn= 1-904994-10-5\n| page= 122}}</ref> and '''AMBA''' (ambient/classical). {{As of|2006}}, Cosmos's \"Take Me With You\" was his most successful track. In 2007, Middleton abandoned the '''AMBA''' moniker, while still focusing on the ambient genre fusing classical traditions with [[electronica]], featuring orchestral, choral and electro acoustic arrangements.  A new EP, [[Excursions 1]] was released on 10 September 2007 while the album [[Lifetracks]] was released on Big Chill Recordings on 1 October 2007 under the name '''Tom Middleton'''.\n\nPredominantly using the Cosmos and Modwheel monikers (and his own name) Middleton has remixed numerous artists including [[Kerri Chandler]], [[Orbital (band)|Orbital]], [[Kylie Minogue]], [[Coldplay]], [[Underworld]], [[Fluke (band)|Fluke]], [[Super Collider]], [[Prince (musician)|Prince]], [[Spiller]], [[Model 500]], [[The Beloved (band)|The Beloved]], [[Rob Dougan]], [[Pulp (band)|Pulp]], [[Leftfield]], [[Saint Etienne (band)|Saint Etienne]], [[Ian Pooley]], [[Dubtribe Sound System]], [[All Saints (band)|All Saints]], [[Goldfrapp]], [[Lamb (band)|Lamb]], [[R\u00f6yksopp]], [[Gotan Project]], [[Amp Fiddler]], [[Mighty Dub Katz]] and [[Bebel Gilberto]]."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"36364898":{"pageid":36364898,"ns":0,"title":"Tommy The latter has reached the top 40 of the [[ARIAnet]] Singles Chart in July 2005, and the top 10 of the [[UK Singles Chart]] in December 2005.<ref name=\"British Hit Singles & Albums\"/>  The song was the 142nd highest selling song of the year in the [[United Kingdom|UK]].<ref>[http://www.ukchartsplus.co.uk/ChartsPlusYE2005.pdf Ukchartplus.co.uk]</ref>\n\nNovy started producing music in 1994 when he signed for the Munich based [[record label]], Kosmo Records, with his first record, \"I House U\", a cover of the [[Jungle Brothers]]' \"I'll House You\", with [[lyrics]] by Novy. He worked variously with [[N-Trance]], [[The Time Frequency]], [[Belinda Carlisle]], [[Ice MC]], [[Scooter (band)|Scooter]], [[Mary Kiani]] and [[DJ Dado]].<ref name=\"Dead\"/> \n\nHis multi-award winning dance music show, ''Steppin' Out'', started in 1985 and ran for fourteen years on [[Radio Forth]], Forth RFM and Forth FM. Although the show was only broadcast to East and Central Scotland, tapes of the show were sent all over the world, hence the reason there were  requests from listeners in [[Australia]], [[Canada]] and [[Hong Kong]]. Due to the success of his show and the Scottish dance music boom, Wilson's ''Bonus Beats'' programme aired on [[Forth One|Forth FM]] during the mid-1990s. The music is written and produced by Jez Willis and Tim Garbutt, who were joined on-stage by other musicians when the band played live from 1991 to 2001, since then they have performed as DJs. The band had three top ten singles in the [[UK Singles Chart]] in the 1990s,<ref name=\"British Hit Singles & Albums\"/> and were notable for their use of [[sampling (music)|sampling]] technology \u2013 in particular, their practice of manipulating samples from mainstream pop and rock songs and combining them with contrasting dance beats, using samples in new contexts. They had 3 further UK top 40 singles in 2000 \u2013 2001, a top 10 single in 2008 and a top 30 single in 2012.\n\nThey have DJed throughout their career, mainly in Europe, USA, Australia and New Zealand averaging a minimum of 80 gigs a year.\n\nDue to their genre crossing sets, Utah Saints have never been fully immersed in any one scene, other than the general electronic dance field. As a result they have performed at a wide range of events, ranging from underground electronic clubs to headlining festival stages, including their legendary headline set at Wickerman Festival in Scotland in 2009, which was nominated as a standout festival moment in the UK festival awards. They also were voted 2nd best dance act at Glastonbury (1st was Fatboy Slim) by NME magazine in 2000."}]}}}}{"query":{"pages":{"2383136":{"pageid":2383136,"ns":0,"title":"Vernessa {{url|http://zedd.net}}}} \n''' Anton Zaslavski ''' ({{lang-ru| \u0410\u043d\u0442\u043e\u043d \u0418\u0433\u043e\u0440\u0435\u0432\u0438\u0447 \u0417\u0430\u0441\u043b\u0430\u0432\u0441\u043a\u0438\u0439}}; born 2 September 1989), better known by his stage name '''Zedd''' ({{IPAc-en|\u02c8|z|\u025b|d}}), is a [[Russians|Russian]]-[[Germans|German]] musician, music producer and DJ.<ref name=\"Allmusic: Zedd (Biography)\">{{cite web | url=http://www.allmusic.com/artist/zedd-mn0002782403/biography| Music|url=http://www.forbes.com/sites/zackomalleygreenburg/2013/08/14/zedd-ahead-meet-the-next-big-star-of-electronic-music/|work=Forbes|accessdate=7 December 2013|date=14 August 2013}}</ref> He primarily produces in the [[electro house]] genre,<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.easyloverecords.com/zeddinterview/ |title=ELR\u2122 Exclusive Interview w/ Zedd &#124 |publisher=Easyloverecords.com |date=19 November 2010 |accessdate=7 November 2012}}</ref> but has branched out, drawing influences from [[progressive house]], [[dubstep]], and [[classical music]]. Zedd grew up and began his career in [[Kaiserslautern]], [[Germany]]. Zedd's best-known productions to date are the songs \"[[Clarity (Zedd song)|Clarity]]\" featuring [[Foxes (singer)|Foxes]] which charted at number 8 on the [[Billboard Hot 100|''Billboard'' Hot 100]] and at number one of the [[Hot Dance Club Songs|US Hot Dance Club Songs]]; and \"[[Break Free (Ariana Grande song)|Break Free]]\", a song which has peaked at number 4 on the [[Billboard Hot 100|''Billboard'' Hot 100]] and number 1 on the [[Hot Dance/Electronic Songs]], becoming his first song to do so. He also won a Grammy award for [[Grammy Award for Best Dance Recording|Best Dance Recording]] at the [[56th Annual Grammy Awards|56th Grammy Awards]] for \"Clarity\".<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/events/grammys-2014/5885369/zedd-cedric-gervais-take-home-first-grammys |title=Zedd & Cedric Gervais Take Home First Grammys |publisher=Billboardy |date=26 January 2014 |accessdate=30 January 2014}}</ref>"}]}}}}[]
